\DoxyCodeLine{3013 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3014 \textcolor{comment}{Fitting by polynomials in barycentric form. This function provides  simple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3015 \textcolor{comment}{unterface for unconstrained unweighted fitting. See  PolynomialFitWC()  if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3016 \textcolor{comment}{you need constrained fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3017 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3018 \textcolor{comment}{The task is linear, thus the linear least  squares  solver  is  used.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3019 \textcolor{comment}{complexity of this computational scheme is O(N*M\string^2), mostly  dominated  by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3020 \textcolor{comment}{the least squares solver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3021 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3022 \textcolor{comment}{SEE ALSO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3023 \textcolor{comment}{    PolynomialFitWC()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3024 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3025 \textcolor{comment}{NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3026 \textcolor{comment}{    you can convert P from barycentric form  to  the  power  or  Chebyshev}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3027 \textcolor{comment}{    basis with PolynomialBar2Pow() or PolynomialBar2Cheb() functions  from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3028 \textcolor{comment}{    POLINT subpackage.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3029 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3030 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3031 \textcolor{comment}{    X   -\/   points, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3032 \textcolor{comment}{    Y   -\/   function values, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3033 \textcolor{comment}{    N   -\/   number of points, N>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3034 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only leading N elements of X/Y are used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3035 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from sizes of X/Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3036 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions (= polynomial\_degree + 1), M>=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3037 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3038 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3041 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info<=0   an error occured:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/4 means inconvergence of internal SVD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043 \textcolor{comment}{    P   -\/   interpolant in barycentric form.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep -\/   report, same format as in LSFitLinearW() subroutine.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3048 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgRelError   average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3049 \textcolor{comment}{            * MaxError      maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3050 \textcolor{comment}{                            NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3051 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3083 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3084 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted  fitting by polynomials in barycentric form, with constraints  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3085 \textcolor{comment}{function values or first derivatives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3086 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3087 \textcolor{comment}{Small regularizing term is used when solving constrained tasks (to improve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3088 \textcolor{comment}{stability).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3089 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090 \textcolor{comment}{Task is linear, so linear least squares solver is used. Complexity of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3091 \textcolor{comment}{computational scheme is O(N*M\string^2), mostly dominated by least squares solver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3092 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3093 \textcolor{comment}{SEE ALSO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3094 \textcolor{comment}{    PolynomialFit()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3095 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3096 \textcolor{comment}{NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3097 \textcolor{comment}{    you can convert P from barycentric form  to  the  power  or  Chebyshev}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098 \textcolor{comment}{    basis with PolynomialBar2Pow() or PolynomialBar2Cheb() functions  from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099 \textcolor{comment}{    POLINT subpackage.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3100 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3101 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3102 \textcolor{comment}{    X   -\/   points, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103 \textcolor{comment}{    Y   -\/   function values, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3104 \textcolor{comment}{    W   -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3105 \textcolor{comment}{            Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation deviations from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3106 \textcolor{comment}{            given  values  is  multiplied  by  the square of corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3107 \textcolor{comment}{            weight. Fill it by 1's if you don't  want  to  solve  weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3108 \textcolor{comment}{            task.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3109 \textcolor{comment}{    N   -\/   number of points, N>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3110 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only leading N elements of X/Y/W are used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3111 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from sizes of X/Y/W}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3112 \textcolor{comment}{    XC  -\/   points where polynomial values/derivatives are constrained,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3113 \textcolor{comment}{            array[0..K-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3114 \textcolor{comment}{    YC  -\/   values of constraints, array[0..K-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3115 \textcolor{comment}{    DC  -\/   array[0..K-\/1], types of constraints:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3116 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=0   means that P(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3117 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=1   means that P'(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3118 \textcolor{comment}{            SEE BELOW FOR IMPORTANT INFORMATION ON CONSTRAINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3119 \textcolor{comment}{    K   -\/   number of constraints, 0<=K<M.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3120 \textcolor{comment}{            K=0 means no constraints (XC/YC/DC are not used in such cases)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3121 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions (= polynomial\_degree + 1), M>=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3122 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3123 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3124 \textcolor{comment}{    Info-\/   same format as in LSFitLinearW() subroutine:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3125 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info>0    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3126 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info<=0   an error occured:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3127 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/4 means inconvergence of internal SVD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3128 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/3 means inconsistent constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3129 \textcolor{comment}{    P   -\/   interpolant in barycentric form.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3130 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep -\/   report, same format as in LSFitLinearW() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3131 \textcolor{comment}{            Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3132 \textcolor{comment}{            * RMSError      rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3133 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgError      average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3134 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgRelError   average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3135 \textcolor{comment}{            * MaxError      maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3136 \textcolor{comment}{                            NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3137 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3138 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3139 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3140 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3141 \textcolor{comment}{SETTING CONSTRAINTS -\/ DANGERS AND OPPORTUNITIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3142 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3143 \textcolor{comment}{Setting constraints can lead  to undesired  results,  like ill-\/conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3144 \textcolor{comment}{behavior, or inconsistency being detected. From the other side,  it allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3145 \textcolor{comment}{us to improve quality of the fit. Here we summarize  our  experience  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3146 \textcolor{comment}{constrained regression splines:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3147 \textcolor{comment}{* even simple constraints can be inconsistent, see  Wikipedia  article  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3148 \textcolor{comment}{  this subject: http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Birkhoff\_interpolation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3149 \textcolor{comment}{* the  greater  is  M (given  fixed  constraints),  the  more chances that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3150 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3151 \textcolor{comment}{* in the general case, consistency of constraints is NOT GUARANTEED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3152 \textcolor{comment}{* in the one special cases, however, we can  guarantee  consistency.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3153 \textcolor{comment}{  case  is:  M>1  and constraints on the function values (NOT DERIVATIVES)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3154 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3155 \textcolor{comment}{Our final recommendation is to use constraints  WHEN  AND  ONLY  when  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3156 \textcolor{comment}{can't solve your task without them. Anything beyond  special  cases  given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3157 \textcolor{comment}{above is not guaranteed and may result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3159 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3160 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3161 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3162 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3163 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3164 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3165 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3166 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3167 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3168 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3169 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3171 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3173 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3183 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3186 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} polynomialfitwc(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&xc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&yc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&dc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t k, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1barycentricinterpolant}{barycentricinterpolant}} \&p, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1polynomialfitreport}{polynomialfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} polynomialfitwc(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&xc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&yc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&dc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1barycentricinterpolant}{barycentricinterpolant}} \&p, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1polynomialfitreport}{polynomialfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3188 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3190 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191 \textcolor{comment}{This function calculates value of four-\/parameter logistic (4PL)  model  at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192 \textcolor{comment}{specified point X. 4PL model has following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D) = D+(A-\/D)/(1+Power(x/C,B))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3195 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   current point, X>=0:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3198 \textcolor{comment}{                * zero X is correctly handled even for B<=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199 \textcolor{comment}{                * negative X results in exception.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3200 \textcolor{comment}{    A, B, C, D-\/ parameters of 4PL model:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201 \textcolor{comment}{                * A is unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3202 \textcolor{comment}{                * B is unconstrained; zero or negative values are handled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3203 \textcolor{comment}{                  correctly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204 \textcolor{comment}{                * C>0, non-\/positive value results in exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3205 \textcolor{comment}{                * D is unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207 \textcolor{comment}{RESULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208 \textcolor{comment}{    model value at X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if B=0, denominator is assumed to be equal to 2.0 even  for  zero  X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211 \textcolor{comment}{      (strictly speaking, 0\string^0 is undefined).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function also throws exception  if  all  input  parameters  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214 \textcolor{comment}{      correct, but overflow was detected during calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function performs a lot of checks;  if  you  need  really  high}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217 \textcolor{comment}{      performance, consider evaluating model  yourself,  without  checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218 \textcolor{comment}{      for degenerate cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.05.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} logisticcalc4(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} b, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} c, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} d, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3226 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3227 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228 \textcolor{comment}{This function calculates value of five-\/parameter logistic (5PL)  model  at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229 \textcolor{comment}{specified point X. 5PL model has following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D,G) = D+(A-\/D)/Power(1+Power(x/C,B),G)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   current point, X>=0:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235 \textcolor{comment}{                * zero X is correctly handled even for B<=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236 \textcolor{comment}{                * negative X results in exception.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237 \textcolor{comment}{    A, B, C, D, G-\/ parameters of 5PL model:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238 \textcolor{comment}{                * A is unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239 \textcolor{comment}{                * B is unconstrained; zero or negative values are handled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240 \textcolor{comment}{                  correctly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241 \textcolor{comment}{                * C>0, non-\/positive value results in exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242 \textcolor{comment}{                * D is unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243 \textcolor{comment}{                * G>0, non-\/positive value results in exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245 \textcolor{comment}{RESULT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246 \textcolor{comment}{    model value at X}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if B=0, denominator is assumed to be equal to Power(2.0,G) even  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249 \textcolor{comment}{      zero X (strictly speaking, 0\string^0 is undefined).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3250 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function also throws exception  if  all  input  parameters  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252 \textcolor{comment}{      correct, but overflow was detected during calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function performs a lot of checks;  if  you  need  really  high}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255 \textcolor{comment}{      performance, consider evaluating model  yourself,  without  checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256 \textcolor{comment}{      for degenerate cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.05.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3262 \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} logisticcalc5(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} a, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} b, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} c, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} d, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} g, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3264 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3265 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266 \textcolor{comment}{This function fits four-\/parameter logistic (4PL) model  to  data  provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3267 \textcolor{comment}{by user. 4PL model has following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D) = D+(A-\/D)/(1+Power(x/C,B))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271 \textcolor{comment}{Here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272 \textcolor{comment}{    * A, D -\/ unconstrained (see LogisticFit4EC() for constrained 4PL)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273 \textcolor{comment}{    * B>=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274 \textcolor{comment}{    * C>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: output of this function is constrained in  such  way that  B>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277 \textcolor{comment}{           Because 4PL model is symmetric with respect to B, there  is  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278 \textcolor{comment}{           need to explore  B<0.  Constraining  B  makes  algorithm easier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279 \textcolor{comment}{           to stabilize and debug.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 \textcolor{comment}{           Users  who  for  some  reason  prefer to work with negative B's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3281 \textcolor{comment}{           should transform output themselves (swap A and D, replace B  by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282 \textcolor{comment}{           -\/B).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3284 \textcolor{comment}{4PL fitting is implemented as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform small number of restarts from random locations which helps to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286 \textcolor{comment}{  solve problem of bad local extrema. Locations are only partially  random}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ we use input data to determine good  initial  guess,  but  we  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288 \textcolor{comment}{  controlled amount of randomness.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3289 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform Levenberg-\/Marquardt fitting with very  tight  constraints  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290 \textcolor{comment}{  parameters B and C -\/ it allows us to find good  initial  guess  for  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3291 \textcolor{comment}{  second stage without risk of running into "{}flat spot"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292 \textcolor{comment}{* second  Levenberg-\/Marquardt  round  is   performed   without   excessive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints. Results from the previous round are used as initial guess.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3294 \textcolor{comment}{* after fitting is done, we compare results with best values found so far,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295 \textcolor{comment}{  rewrite "{}best solution"{} if needed, and move to next random location.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3296 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297 \textcolor{comment}{Overall algorithm is very stable and is not prone to  bad  local  extrema.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298 \textcolor{comment}{Furthermore, it automatically scales when input data have  very  large  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299 \textcolor{comment}{very small range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3300 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], stores X-\/values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3303 \textcolor{comment}{                MUST include only non-\/negative numbers  (but  may  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3304 \textcolor{comment}{                zero values). Can be unsorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3305 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[N], values to fit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3306 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points. If N is less than  length  of  X/Y, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3307 \textcolor{comment}{                leading N elements are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3308 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3309 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310 \textcolor{comment}{    A, B, C, D-\/ parameters of 4PL model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. This structure has many fields,  but  ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3312 \textcolor{comment}{                ONES LISTED BELOW ARE SET:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3313 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount -\/ number of iterations performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3314 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.RMSError -\/ root-\/mean-\/square error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgError -\/ average absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgRelError -\/ average relative error (calculated for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317 \textcolor{comment}{                  non-\/zero Y-\/values)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3318 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxError -\/ maximum absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3319 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 -\/ coefficient of determination,  R-\/squared.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3320 \textcolor{comment}{                  coefficient   is  calculated  as  R2=1-\/RSS/TSS  (in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3321 \textcolor{comment}{                  of nonlinear  regression  there  are  multiple  ways  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3322 \textcolor{comment}{                  define R2, each of them giving different results).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3323 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3324 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: for stability reasons the B parameter is restricted by [1/1000,1000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3325 \textcolor{comment}{      range. It prevents  algorithm from making trial steps  deep into the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3326 \textcolor{comment}{      area of bad parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3327 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3328 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: after  you  obtained  coefficients,  you  can  evaluate  model  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3329 \textcolor{comment}{      LogisticCalc4() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3330 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3331 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need better control over fitting process than provided by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3332 \textcolor{comment}{      function, you may use LogisticFit45X().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3333 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3334 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: step is automatically scaled according to scale of parameters  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3335 \textcolor{comment}{      fitted before we compare its length with EpsX. Thus,  this  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3336 \textcolor{comment}{      can be used to fit data with very small or very large values without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3337 \textcolor{comment}{      changing EpsX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3338 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3339 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3340 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3341 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3342 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3343 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} logisticfit4(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&d, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3344 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3345 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3346 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3347 \textcolor{comment}{This function fits four-\/parameter logistic (4PL) model  to  data  provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3348 \textcolor{comment}{by user, with optional constraints on parameters A and D.  4PL  model  has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3349 \textcolor{comment}{following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3350 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3351 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D) = D+(A-\/D)/(1+Power(x/C,B))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3352 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3353 \textcolor{comment}{Here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3354 \textcolor{comment}{    * A, D -\/ with optional equality constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3355 \textcolor{comment}{    * B>=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3356 \textcolor{comment}{    * C>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3357 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3358 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: output of this function is constrained in  such  way that  B>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3359 \textcolor{comment}{           Because 4PL model is symmetric with respect to B, there  is  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3360 \textcolor{comment}{           need to explore  B<0.  Constraining  B  makes  algorithm easier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3361 \textcolor{comment}{           to stabilize and debug.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3362 \textcolor{comment}{           Users  who  for  some  reason  prefer to work with negative B's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3363 \textcolor{comment}{           should transform output themselves (swap A and D, replace B  by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3364 \textcolor{comment}{           -\/B).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3365 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366 \textcolor{comment}{4PL fitting is implemented as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform small number of restarts from random locations which helps to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3368 \textcolor{comment}{  solve problem of bad local extrema. Locations are only partially  random}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ we use input data to determine good  initial  guess,  but  we  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370 \textcolor{comment}{  controlled amount of randomness.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform Levenberg-\/Marquardt fitting with very  tight  constraints  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372 \textcolor{comment}{  parameters B and C -\/ it allows us to find good  initial  guess  for  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3373 \textcolor{comment}{  second stage without risk of running into "{}flat spot"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3374 \textcolor{comment}{* second  Levenberg-\/Marquardt  round  is   performed   without   excessive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints. Results from the previous round are used as initial guess.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376 \textcolor{comment}{* after fitting is done, we compare results with best values found so far,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377 \textcolor{comment}{  rewrite "{}best solution"{} if needed, and move to next random location.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3378 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3379 \textcolor{comment}{Overall algorithm is very stable and is not prone to  bad  local  extrema.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3380 \textcolor{comment}{Furthermore, it automatically scales when input data have  very  large  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3381 \textcolor{comment}{very small range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3382 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3383 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3384 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], stores X-\/values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3385 \textcolor{comment}{                MUST include only non-\/negative numbers  (but  may  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3386 \textcolor{comment}{                zero values). Can be unsorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3387 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[N], values to fit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3388 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points. If N is less than  length  of  X/Y, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3389 \textcolor{comment}{                leading N elements are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3390 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrLeft-\/  optional equality constraint for model value at the   left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3391 \textcolor{comment}{                boundary (at X=0). Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number)  if  you  do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3392 \textcolor{comment}{                not need constraint on the model value at X=0 (in C++  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393 \textcolor{comment}{                can pass alglib::fp\_nan as parameter, in  C\#  it  will  be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394 \textcolor{comment}{                Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3396 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrRight-\/ optional equality constraint for model value at X=infinity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3398 \textcolor{comment}{                Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number) if you do not  need  constraint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3399 \textcolor{comment}{                on the model value (in C++  you can pass alglib::fp\_nan as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400 \textcolor{comment}{                parameter, in  C\# it will  be Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3404 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405 \textcolor{comment}{    A, B, C, D-\/ parameters of 4PL model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3406 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. This structure has many fields,  but  ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3407 \textcolor{comment}{                ONES LISTED BELOW ARE SET:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3408 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount -\/ number of iterations performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3409 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.RMSError -\/ root-\/mean-\/square error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgError -\/ average absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgRelError -\/ average relative error (calculated for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3412 \textcolor{comment}{                  non-\/zero Y-\/values)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3413 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxError -\/ maximum absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3414 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 -\/ coefficient of determination,  R-\/squared.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415 \textcolor{comment}{                  coefficient   is  calculated  as  R2=1-\/RSS/TSS  (in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416 \textcolor{comment}{                  of nonlinear  regression  there  are  multiple  ways  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417 \textcolor{comment}{                  define R2, each of them giving different results).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3418 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: for stability reasons the B parameter is restricted by [1/1000,1000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420 \textcolor{comment}{      range. It prevents  algorithm from making trial steps  deep into the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421 \textcolor{comment}{      area of bad parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: after  you  obtained  coefficients,  you  can  evaluate  model  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424 \textcolor{comment}{      LogisticCalc4() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need better control over fitting process than provided by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427 \textcolor{comment}{      function, you may use LogisticFit45X().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: step is automatically scaled according to scale of parameters  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430 \textcolor{comment}{      fitted before we compare its length with EpsX. Thus,  this  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431 \textcolor{comment}{      can be used to fit data with very small or very large values without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432 \textcolor{comment}{      changing EpsX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434 \textcolor{comment}{EQUALITY CONSTRAINTS ON PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436 \textcolor{comment}{4PL/5PL solver supports equality constraints on model values at  the  left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437 \textcolor{comment}{boundary (X=0) and right  boundary  (X=infinity).  These  constraints  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438 \textcolor{comment}{completely optional and you can specify both of them, only  one  -\/  or  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439 \textcolor{comment}{constraints at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441 \textcolor{comment}{Parameter  CnstrLeft  contains  left  constraint (or NAN for unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442 \textcolor{comment}{fitting), and CnstrRight contains right  one.  For  4PL,  left  constraint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443 \textcolor{comment}{ALWAYS corresponds to parameter A, and right one is ALWAYS  constraint  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 \textcolor{comment}{D. That's because 4PL model is normalized in such way that B>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} logisticfit4ec(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrleft, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrright, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&d, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3453 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454 \textcolor{comment}{This function fits five-\/parameter logistic (5PL) model  to  data  provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455 \textcolor{comment}{by user. 5PL model has following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3457 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D,G) = D+(A-\/D)/Power(1+Power(x/C,B),G)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459 \textcolor{comment}{Here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460 \textcolor{comment}{    * A, D -\/ unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461 \textcolor{comment}{    * B -\/ unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462 \textcolor{comment}{    * C>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3463 \textcolor{comment}{    * G>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: unlike in  4PL  fitting,  output  of  this  function   is   NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466 \textcolor{comment}{           constrained in  such  way that B is guaranteed to be  positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467 \textcolor{comment}{           Furthermore,  unlike  4PL,  5PL  model  is  NOT  symmetric with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468 \textcolor{comment}{           respect to B, so you can NOT transform model to equivalent one,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469 \textcolor{comment}{           with B having desired sign (>0 or <0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471 \textcolor{comment}{5PL fitting is implemented as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform small number of restarts from random locations which helps to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473 \textcolor{comment}{  solve problem of bad local extrema. Locations are only partially  random}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ we use input data to determine good  initial  guess,  but  we  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475 \textcolor{comment}{  controlled amount of randomness.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform Levenberg-\/Marquardt fitting with very  tight  constraints  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477 \textcolor{comment}{  parameters B and C -\/ it allows us to find good  initial  guess  for  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478 \textcolor{comment}{  second stage without risk of running into "{}flat spot"{}.  Parameter  G  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479 \textcolor{comment}{  fixed at G=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480 \textcolor{comment}{* second  Levenberg-\/Marquardt  round  is   performed   without   excessive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints on B and C, but with G still equal to 1.  Results  from  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482 \textcolor{comment}{  previous round are used as initial guess.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483 \textcolor{comment}{* third Levenberg-\/Marquardt round relaxes constraints on G  and  tries  two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 \textcolor{comment}{  different models -\/ one with B>0 and one with B<0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485 \textcolor{comment}{* after fitting is done, we compare results with best values found so far,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486 \textcolor{comment}{  rewrite "{}best solution"{} if needed, and move to next random location.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488 \textcolor{comment}{Overall algorithm is very stable and is not prone to  bad  local  extrema.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489 \textcolor{comment}{Furthermore, it automatically scales when input data have  very  large  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490 \textcolor{comment}{very small range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], stores X-\/values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494 \textcolor{comment}{                MUST include only non-\/negative numbers  (but  may  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495 \textcolor{comment}{                zero values). Can be unsorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[N], values to fit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points. If N is less than  length  of  X/Y, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498 \textcolor{comment}{                leading N elements are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501 \textcolor{comment}{    A,B,C,D,G-\/  parameters of 5PL model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. This structure has many fields,  but  ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503 \textcolor{comment}{                ONES LISTED BELOW ARE SET:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount -\/ number of iterations performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.RMSError -\/ root-\/mean-\/square error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgError -\/ average absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgRelError -\/ average relative error (calculated for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508 \textcolor{comment}{                  non-\/zero Y-\/values)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxError -\/ maximum absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 -\/ coefficient of determination,  R-\/squared.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511 \textcolor{comment}{                  coefficient   is  calculated  as  R2=1-\/RSS/TSS  (in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512 \textcolor{comment}{                  of nonlinear  regression  there  are  multiple  ways  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513 \textcolor{comment}{                  define R2, each of them giving different results).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: for better stability B  parameter is restricted by [+-\/1/1000,+-\/1000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516 \textcolor{comment}{      range, and G is restricted by [1/10,10] range. It prevents algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517 \textcolor{comment}{      from making trial steps deep into the area of bad parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3518 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: after  you  obtained  coefficients,  you  can  evaluate  model  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3520 \textcolor{comment}{      LogisticCalc5() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need better control over fitting process than provided by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523 \textcolor{comment}{      function, you may use LogisticFit45X().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: step is automatically scaled according to scale of parameters  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526 \textcolor{comment}{      fitted before we compare its length with EpsX. Thus,  this  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527 \textcolor{comment}{      can be used to fit data with very small or very large values without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528 \textcolor{comment}{      changing EpsX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} logisticfit5(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&d, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&g, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3536 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3537 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538 \textcolor{comment}{This function fits five-\/parameter logistic (5PL) model  to  data  provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539 \textcolor{comment}{by user, subject to optional equality constraints on parameters A  and  D.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540 \textcolor{comment}{5PL model has following form:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D,G) = D+(A-\/D)/Power(1+Power(x/C,B),G)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544 \textcolor{comment}{Here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545 \textcolor{comment}{    * A, D -\/ with optional equality constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546 \textcolor{comment}{    * B -\/ unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547 \textcolor{comment}{    * C>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548 \textcolor{comment}{    * G>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: unlike in  4PL  fitting,  output  of  this  function   is   NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551 \textcolor{comment}{           constrained in  such  way that B is guaranteed to be  positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3552 \textcolor{comment}{           Furthermore,  unlike  4PL,  5PL  model  is  NOT  symmetric with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3553 \textcolor{comment}{           respect to B, so you can NOT transform model to equivalent one,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3554 \textcolor{comment}{           with B having desired sign (>0 or <0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556 \textcolor{comment}{5PL fitting is implemented as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform small number of restarts from random locations which helps to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558 \textcolor{comment}{  solve problem of bad local extrema. Locations are only partially  random}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ we use input data to determine good  initial  guess,  but  we  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3560 \textcolor{comment}{  controlled amount of randomness.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3561 \textcolor{comment}{* we perform Levenberg-\/Marquardt fitting with very  tight  constraints  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3562 \textcolor{comment}{  parameters B and C -\/ it allows us to find good  initial  guess  for  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3563 \textcolor{comment}{  second stage without risk of running into "{}flat spot"{}.  Parameter  G  is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3564 \textcolor{comment}{  fixed at G=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3565 \textcolor{comment}{* second  Levenberg-\/Marquardt  round  is   performed   without   excessive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints on B and C, but with G still equal to 1.  Results  from  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3567 \textcolor{comment}{  previous round are used as initial guess.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3568 \textcolor{comment}{* third Levenberg-\/Marquardt round relaxes constraints on G  and  tries  two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3569 \textcolor{comment}{  different models -\/ one with B>0 and one with B<0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570 \textcolor{comment}{* after fitting is done, we compare results with best values found so far,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571 \textcolor{comment}{  rewrite "{}best solution"{} if needed, and move to next random location.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3573 \textcolor{comment}{Overall algorithm is very stable and is not prone to  bad  local  extrema.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574 \textcolor{comment}{Furthermore, it automatically scales when input data have  very  large  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575 \textcolor{comment}{very small range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3577 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3578 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], stores X-\/values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579 \textcolor{comment}{                MUST include only non-\/negative numbers  (but  may  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580 \textcolor{comment}{                zero values). Can be unsorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[N], values to fit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3582 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points. If N is less than  length  of  X/Y, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3583 \textcolor{comment}{                leading N elements are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3584 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrLeft-\/  optional equality constraint for model value at the   left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3585 \textcolor{comment}{                boundary (at X=0). Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number)  if  you  do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586 \textcolor{comment}{                not need constraint on the model value at X=0 (in C++  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3587 \textcolor{comment}{                can pass alglib::fp\_nan as parameter, in  C\#  it  will  be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588 \textcolor{comment}{                Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3590 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3591 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrRight-\/ optional equality constraint for model value at X=infinity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592 \textcolor{comment}{                Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number) if you do not  need  constraint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593 \textcolor{comment}{                on the model value (in C++  you can pass alglib::fp\_nan as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3594 \textcolor{comment}{                parameter, in  C\# it will  be Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3595 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3597 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599 \textcolor{comment}{    A,B,C,D,G-\/  parameters of 5PL model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. This structure has many fields,  but  ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601 \textcolor{comment}{                ONES LISTED BELOW ARE SET:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount -\/ number of iterations performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3603 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.RMSError -\/ root-\/mean-\/square error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgError -\/ average absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgRelError -\/ average relative error (calculated for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3606 \textcolor{comment}{                  non-\/zero Y-\/values)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxError -\/ maximum absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 -\/ coefficient of determination,  R-\/squared.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609 \textcolor{comment}{                  coefficient   is  calculated  as  R2=1-\/RSS/TSS  (in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610 \textcolor{comment}{                  of nonlinear  regression  there  are  multiple  ways  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3611 \textcolor{comment}{                  define R2, each of them giving different results).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: for better stability B  parameter is restricted by [+-\/1/1000,+-\/1000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614 \textcolor{comment}{      range, and G is restricted by [1/10,10] range. It prevents algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615 \textcolor{comment}{      from making trial steps deep into the area of bad parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: after  you  obtained  coefficients,  you  can  evaluate  model  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618 \textcolor{comment}{      LogisticCalc5() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need better control over fitting process than provided by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621 \textcolor{comment}{      function, you may use LogisticFit45X().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: step is automatically scaled according to scale of parameters  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624 \textcolor{comment}{      fitted before we compare its length with EpsX. Thus,  this  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625 \textcolor{comment}{      can be used to fit data with very small or very large values without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626 \textcolor{comment}{      changing EpsX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628 \textcolor{comment}{EQUALITY CONSTRAINTS ON PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630 \textcolor{comment}{5PL solver supports equality constraints on model  values  at   the   left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631 \textcolor{comment}{boundary (X=0) and right  boundary  (X=infinity).  These  constraints  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632 \textcolor{comment}{completely optional and you can specify both of them, only  one  -\/  or  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633 \textcolor{comment}{constraints at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635 \textcolor{comment}{Parameter  CnstrLeft  contains  left  constraint (or NAN for unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3636 \textcolor{comment}{fitting), and CnstrRight contains right  one.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3638 \textcolor{comment}{Unlike 4PL one, 5PL model is NOT symmetric with respect to  change in sign}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3639 \textcolor{comment}{of B. Thus, negative B's are possible, and left constraint  may  constrain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3640 \textcolor{comment}{parameter A (for positive B's)  -\/  or  parameter  D  (for  negative  B's).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641 \textcolor{comment}{Similarly changes meaning of right constraint.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3643 \textcolor{comment}{You do not have to decide what parameter to  constrain  -\/  algorithm  will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644 \textcolor{comment}{automatically determine correct parameters as fitting progresses. However,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645 \textcolor{comment}{question highlighted above is important when you interpret fitting results.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} logisticfit5ec(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrleft, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrright, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&d, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&g, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3652 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3654 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655 \textcolor{comment}{This is "{}expert"{} 4PL/5PL fitting function, which can be used if  you  need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656 \textcolor{comment}{better control over fitting process than provided  by  LogisticFit4()  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657 \textcolor{comment}{LogisticFit5().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659 \textcolor{comment}{This function fits model of the form}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D)   = D+(A-\/D)/(1+Power(x/C,B))           (4PL model)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663 \textcolor{comment}{or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665 \textcolor{comment}{    F(x|A,B,C,D,G) = D+(A-\/D)/Power(1+Power(x/C,B),G)    (5PL model)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667 \textcolor{comment}{Here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668 \textcolor{comment}{    * A, D -\/ unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669 \textcolor{comment}{    * B>=0 for 4PL, unconstrained for 5PL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670 \textcolor{comment}{    * C>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671 \textcolor{comment}{    * G>0 (if present)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[N], stores X-\/values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3675 \textcolor{comment}{                MUST include only non-\/negative numbers  (but  may  include}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676 \textcolor{comment}{                zero values). Can be unsorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[N], values to fit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points. If N is less than  length  of  X/Y, only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679 \textcolor{comment}{                leading N elements are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrLeft-\/  optional equality constraint for model value at the   left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681 \textcolor{comment}{                boundary (at X=0). Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number)  if  you  do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682 \textcolor{comment}{                not need constraint on the model value at X=0 (in C++  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683 \textcolor{comment}{                can pass alglib::fp\_nan as parameter, in  C\#  it  will  be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684 \textcolor{comment}{                Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687 \textcolor{comment}{    CnstrRight-\/ optional equality constraint for model value at X=infinity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688 \textcolor{comment}{                Specify NAN (Not-\/a-\/Number) if you do not  need  constraint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689 \textcolor{comment}{                on the model value (in C++  you can pass alglib::fp\_nan as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690 \textcolor{comment}{                parameter, in  C\# it will  be Double.NaN).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691 \textcolor{comment}{                See  below,  section  "{}EQUALITY  CONSTRAINTS"{}   for   more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692 \textcolor{comment}{                information about constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693 \textcolor{comment}{    Is4PL   -\/   whether 4PL or 5PL models are fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694 \textcolor{comment}{    LambdaV -\/   regularization coefficient, LambdaV>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 \textcolor{comment}{                Set it to zero unless you know what you are doing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696 \textcolor{comment}{    EpsX    -\/   stopping condition (step size), EpsX>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697 \textcolor{comment}{                Zero value means that small step is automatically chosen.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698 \textcolor{comment}{                See notes below for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699 \textcolor{comment}{    RsCnt   -\/   number of repeated restarts from  random  points.  4PL/5PL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700 \textcolor{comment}{                models are prone to problem of bad local extrema. Utilizing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701 \textcolor{comment}{                multiple random restarts allows  us  to  improve algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702 \textcolor{comment}{                convergence.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703 \textcolor{comment}{                RsCnt>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704 \textcolor{comment}{                Zero value means that function automatically choose  small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705 \textcolor{comment}{                amount of restarts (recommended).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708 \textcolor{comment}{    A, B, C, D-\/ parameters of 4PL model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709 \textcolor{comment}{    G       -\/   parameter of 5PL model; for Is4PL=True, G=1 is returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. This structure has many fields,  but  ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3711 \textcolor{comment}{                ONES LISTED BELOW ARE SET:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3712 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.IterationsCount -\/ number of iterations performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3713 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.RMSError -\/ root-\/mean-\/square error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3714 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgError -\/ average absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3715 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.AvgRelError -\/ average relative error (calculated for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3716 \textcolor{comment}{                  non-\/zero Y-\/values)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3717 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.MaxError -\/ maximum absolute error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3718 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.R2 -\/ coefficient of determination,  R-\/squared.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3719 \textcolor{comment}{                  coefficient   is  calculated  as  R2=1-\/RSS/TSS  (in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3720 \textcolor{comment}{                  of nonlinear  regression  there  are  multiple  ways  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3721 \textcolor{comment}{                  define R2, each of them giving different results).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3722 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3723 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: for better stability B  parameter is restricted by [+-\/1/1000,+-\/1000]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3724 \textcolor{comment}{      range, and G is restricted by [1/10,10] range. It prevents algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3725 \textcolor{comment}{      from making trial steps deep into the area of bad parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3726 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3727 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: after  you  obtained  coefficients,  you  can  evaluate  model  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3728 \textcolor{comment}{      LogisticCalc5() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3729 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3730 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: step is automatically scaled according to scale of parameters  being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3731 \textcolor{comment}{      fitted before we compare its length with EpsX. Thus,  this  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3732 \textcolor{comment}{      can be used to fit data with very small or very large values without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3733 \textcolor{comment}{      changing EpsX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3734 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3735 \textcolor{comment}{EQUALITY CONSTRAINTS ON PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3736 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3737 \textcolor{comment}{4PL/5PL solver supports equality constraints on model values at  the  left}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3738 \textcolor{comment}{boundary (X=0) and right  boundary  (X=infinity).  These  constraints  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3739 \textcolor{comment}{completely optional and you can specify both of them, only  one  -\/  or  no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3740 \textcolor{comment}{constraints at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3741 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3742 \textcolor{comment}{Parameter  CnstrLeft  contains  left  constraint (or NAN for unconstrained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3743 \textcolor{comment}{fitting), and CnstrRight contains right  one.  For  4PL,  left  constraint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3744 \textcolor{comment}{ALWAYS corresponds to parameter A, and right one is ALWAYS  constraint  on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3745 \textcolor{comment}{D. That's because 4PL model is normalized in such way that B>=0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3746 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3747 \textcolor{comment}{For 5PL model things are different. Unlike  4PL  one,  5PL  model  is  NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3748 \textcolor{comment}{symmetric with respect to  change  in  sign  of  B. Thus, negative B's are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3749 \textcolor{comment}{possible, and left constraint may constrain parameter A (for positive B's)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3750 \textcolor{comment}{-\/ or parameter D (for negative B's). Similarly changes  meaning  of  right}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3751 \textcolor{comment}{constraint.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3752 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3753 \textcolor{comment}{You do not have to decide what parameter to  constrain  -\/  algorithm  will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3754 \textcolor{comment}{automatically determine correct parameters as fitting progresses. However,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3755 \textcolor{comment}{question highlighted above is important when you interpret fitting results.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3756 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3757 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3758 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB PROJECT -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3759 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 14.02.2014 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3760 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3761 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} logisticfit45x(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrleft, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} cnstrright, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} is4pl, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} lambdav, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} epsx, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t rscnt, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&d, \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} \&g, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3762 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3763 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3764 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3765 \textcolor{comment}{Weghted rational least  squares  fitting  using  Floater-\/Hormann  rational}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3766 \textcolor{comment}{functions  with  optimal  D  chosen  from  [0,9],  with  constraints   and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3767 \textcolor{comment}{individual weights.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3768 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3769 \textcolor{comment}{Equidistant  grid  with M node on [min(x),max(x)]  is  used to build basis}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3770 \textcolor{comment}{functions. Different values of D are tried, optimal D (least WEIGHTED root}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3771 \textcolor{comment}{mean square error) is chosen.  Task  is  linear,  so  linear least squares}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3772 \textcolor{comment}{solver  is  used.  Complexity  of  this  computational  scheme is O(N*M\string^2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3773 \textcolor{comment}{(mostly dominated by the least squares solver).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3774 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3775 \textcolor{comment}{SEE ALSO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3776 \textcolor{comment}{* BarycentricFitFloaterHormann(), "{}lightweight"{} fitting without invididual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3777 \textcolor{comment}{  weights and constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3778 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3779 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3780 \textcolor{comment}{    X   -\/   points, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3781 \textcolor{comment}{    Y   -\/   function values, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3782 \textcolor{comment}{    W   -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3783 \textcolor{comment}{            Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation deviations from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3784 \textcolor{comment}{            given  values  is  multiplied  by  the square of corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3785 \textcolor{comment}{            weight. Fill it by 1's if you don't  want  to  solve  weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3786 \textcolor{comment}{            task.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3787 \textcolor{comment}{    N   -\/   number of points, N>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3788 \textcolor{comment}{    XC  -\/   points where function values/derivatives are constrained,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3789 \textcolor{comment}{            array[0..K-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3790 \textcolor{comment}{    YC  -\/   values of constraints, array[0..K-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3791 \textcolor{comment}{    DC  -\/   array[0..K-\/1], types of constraints:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3792 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=0   means that S(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3793 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=1   means that S'(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3794 \textcolor{comment}{            SEE BELOW FOR IMPORTANT INFORMATION ON CONSTRAINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3795 \textcolor{comment}{    K   -\/   number of constraints, 0<=K<M.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3796 \textcolor{comment}{            K=0 means no constraints (XC/YC/DC are not used in such cases)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3797 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions ( = number\_of\_nodes), M>=2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3798 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3799 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3800 \textcolor{comment}{    Info-\/   same format as in LSFitLinearWC() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3801 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info>0    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3802 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info<=0   an error occured:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3803 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/4 means inconvergence of internal SVD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3804 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/3 means inconsistent constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3805 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/1 means another errors in parameters passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3806 \textcolor{comment}{                           (N<=0, for example)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3807 \textcolor{comment}{    B   -\/   barycentric interpolant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3808 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep -\/   report, same format as in LSFitLinearWC() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3809 \textcolor{comment}{            Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3810 \textcolor{comment}{            * DBest         best value of the D parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3811 \textcolor{comment}{            * RMSError      rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3812 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgError      average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3813 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgRelError   average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3814 \textcolor{comment}{            * MaxError      maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3815 \textcolor{comment}{                            NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3816 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3817 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3818 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroutine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3819 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3820 \textcolor{comment}{SETTING CONSTRAINTS -\/ DANGERS AND OPPORTUNITIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3821 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3822 \textcolor{comment}{Setting constraints can lead  to undesired  results,  like ill-\/conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3823 \textcolor{comment}{behavior, or inconsistency being detected. From the other side,  it allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3824 \textcolor{comment}{us to improve quality of the fit. Here we summarize  our  experience  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3825 \textcolor{comment}{constrained barycentric interpolants:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3826 \textcolor{comment}{* excessive  constraints  can  be  inconsistent.   Floater-\/Hormann   basis}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3827 \textcolor{comment}{  functions aren't as flexible as splines (although they are very smooth).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3828 \textcolor{comment}{* the more evenly constraints are spread across [min(x),max(x)],  the more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3829 \textcolor{comment}{  chances that they will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3830 \textcolor{comment}{* the  greater  is  M (given  fixed  constraints),  the  more chances that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3831 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3832 \textcolor{comment}{* in the general case, consistency of constraints IS NOT GUARANTEED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3833 \textcolor{comment}{* in the several special cases, however, we CAN guarantee consistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3834 \textcolor{comment}{* one of this cases is constraints on the function  VALUES at the interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3835 \textcolor{comment}{  boundaries. Note that consustency of the  constraints  on  the  function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3836 \textcolor{comment}{  DERIVATIVES is NOT guaranteed (you can use in such cases  cubic  splines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3837 \textcolor{comment}{  which are more flexible).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3838 \textcolor{comment}{* another  special  case  is ONE constraint on the function value (OR, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3839 \textcolor{comment}{  not AND, derivative) anywhere in the interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3840 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3841 \textcolor{comment}{Our final recommendation is to use constraints  WHEN  AND  ONLY  WHEN  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3842 \textcolor{comment}{can't solve your task without them. Anything beyond  special  cases  given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3843 \textcolor{comment}{above is not guaranteed and may result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3844 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3845 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3846 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3847 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3848 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3849 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3850 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3851 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3852 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3853 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3854 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3855 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3867 \textcolor{comment}{  ! related features provided by commercial edition of ALGLIB.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3875 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3876 \textcolor{comment}{Rational least squares fitting using  Floater-\/Hormann  rational  functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3877 \textcolor{comment}{with optimal D chosen from [0,9].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3878 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3880 \textcolor{comment}{functions. Different values of D are tried, optimal  D  (least  root  mean}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3881 \textcolor{comment}{square error) is chosen.  Task  is  linear, so linear least squares solver}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3889 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions ( = number\_of\_nodes), M>=2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3890 \textcolor{comment}{}}
