\DoxyCodeLine{3934 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} barycentricfitfloaterhormann(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1barycentricinterpolant}{barycentricinterpolant}} \&b, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1barycentricfitreport}{barycentricfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3935 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3936 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3937 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3938 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted fitting by cubic  spline,  with constraints on function values or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3939 \textcolor{comment}{derivatives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3940 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3941 \textcolor{comment}{Equidistant grid with M-\/2 nodes on [min(x,xc),max(x,xc)] is  used to build}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3942 \textcolor{comment}{basis functions. Basis functions are cubic splines with continuous  second}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3943 \textcolor{comment}{derivatives  and  non-\/fixed first  derivatives  at  interval  ends.  Small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3944 \textcolor{comment}{regularizing term is used  when  solving  constrained  tasks  (to  improve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3945 \textcolor{comment}{stability).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3946 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3947 \textcolor{comment}{Task is linear, so linear least squares solver is used. Complexity of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3948 \textcolor{comment}{computational scheme is O(N*M\string^2), mostly dominated by least squares solver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3949 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3950 \textcolor{comment}{SEE ALSO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3951 \textcolor{comment}{    Spline1DFitHermiteWC()  -\/   fitting by Hermite splines (more flexible,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3952 \textcolor{comment}{                                less smooth)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3953 \textcolor{comment}{    Spline1DFitCubic()      -\/   "{}lightweight"{} fitting  by  cubic  splines,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3954 \textcolor{comment}{                                without invididual weights and constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3955 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3956 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3957 \textcolor{comment}{    X   -\/   points, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3958 \textcolor{comment}{    Y   -\/   function values, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3959 \textcolor{comment}{    W   -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3960 \textcolor{comment}{            Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation deviations from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3961 \textcolor{comment}{            given  values  is  multiplied  by  the square of corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962 \textcolor{comment}{            weight. Fill it by 1's if you don't  want  to  solve  weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3963 \textcolor{comment}{            task.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964 \textcolor{comment}{    N   -\/   number of points (optional):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3965 \textcolor{comment}{            * N>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only first N elements of X/Y/W are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3967 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from X/Y/W sizes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3968 \textcolor{comment}{    XC  -\/   points where spline values/derivatives are constrained,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969 \textcolor{comment}{            array[0..K-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3970 \textcolor{comment}{    YC  -\/   values of constraints, array[0..K-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3971 \textcolor{comment}{    DC  -\/   array[0..K-\/1], types of constraints:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=0   means that S(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3973 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=1   means that S'(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3974 \textcolor{comment}{            SEE BELOW FOR IMPORTANT INFORMATION ON CONSTRAINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975 \textcolor{comment}{    K   -\/   number of constraints (optional):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976 \textcolor{comment}{            * 0<=K<M.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3977 \textcolor{comment}{            * K=0 means no constraints (XC/YC/DC are not used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3978 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only first K elements of XC/YC/DC are used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3979 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from XC/YC/DC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions ( = number\_of\_nodes+2), M>=4.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3982 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3983 \textcolor{comment}{    Info-\/   same format as in LSFitLinearWC() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3984 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info>0    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3985 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info<=0   an error occured:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/4 means inconvergence of internal SVD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/3 means inconsistent constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3988 \textcolor{comment}{    S   -\/   spline interpolant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep -\/   report, same format as in LSFitLinearWC() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990 \textcolor{comment}{            Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3991 \textcolor{comment}{            * RMSError      rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3992 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgError      average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgRelError   average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994 \textcolor{comment}{            * MaxError      maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995 \textcolor{comment}{                            NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3997 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3998 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3999 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4000 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4001 \textcolor{comment}{ORDER OF POINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003 \textcolor{comment}{Subroutine automatically sorts points, so caller may pass unsorted array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4005 \textcolor{comment}{SETTING CONSTRAINTS -\/ DANGERS AND OPPORTUNITIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4007 \textcolor{comment}{Setting constraints can lead  to undesired  results,  like ill-\/conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4008 \textcolor{comment}{behavior, or inconsistency being detected. From the other side,  it allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4009 \textcolor{comment}{us to improve quality of the fit. Here we summarize  our  experience  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4010 \textcolor{comment}{constrained regression splines:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4011 \textcolor{comment}{* excessive constraints can be inconsistent. Splines are  piecewise  cubic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4012 \textcolor{comment}{  functions, and it is easy to create an example, where  large  number  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4013 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints  concentrated  in  small  area will result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4014 \textcolor{comment}{  Just because spline is not flexible enough to satisfy all of  them.  And}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4015 \textcolor{comment}{  same constraints spread across the  [min(x),max(x)]  will  be  perfectly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4016 \textcolor{comment}{  consistent.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4017 \textcolor{comment}{* the more evenly constraints are spread across [min(x),max(x)],  the more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4018 \textcolor{comment}{  chances that they will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4019 \textcolor{comment}{* the  greater  is  M (given  fixed  constraints),  the  more chances that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4020 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4021 \textcolor{comment}{* in the general case, consistency of constraints IS NOT GUARANTEED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4022 \textcolor{comment}{* in the several special cases, however, we CAN guarantee consistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4023 \textcolor{comment}{* one of this cases is constraints  on  the  function  values  AND/OR  its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4024 \textcolor{comment}{  derivatives at the interval boundaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4025 \textcolor{comment}{* another  special  case  is ONE constraint on the function value (OR, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4026 \textcolor{comment}{  not AND, derivative) anywhere in the interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4027 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4028 \textcolor{comment}{Our final recommendation is to use constraints  WHEN  AND  ONLY  WHEN  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4029 \textcolor{comment}{can't solve your task without them. Anything beyond  special  cases  given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4030 \textcolor{comment}{above is not guaranteed and may result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4031 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4032 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4033 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4034 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4059 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} spline1dfitcubicwc(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&xc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&yc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&dc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t k, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1spline1dinterpolant}{spline1dinterpolant}} \&s, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1spline1dfitreport}{spline1dfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} spline1dfitcubicwc(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&xc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&yc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1integer__1d__array}{integer\_1d\_array}} \&dc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1spline1dinterpolant}{spline1dinterpolant}} \&s, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1spline1dfitreport}{spline1dfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4062 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4063 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted  fitting  by Hermite spline,  with constraints on function values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4065 \textcolor{comment}{or first derivatives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067 \textcolor{comment}{Equidistant grid with M nodes on [min(x,xc),max(x,xc)] is  used  to  build}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068 \textcolor{comment}{basis functions. Basis functions are Hermite splines.  Small  regularizing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069 \textcolor{comment}{term is used when solving constrained tasks (to improve stability).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4071 \textcolor{comment}{Task is linear, so linear least squares solver is used. Complexity of this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4072 \textcolor{comment}{computational scheme is O(N*M\string^2), mostly dominated by least squares solver}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4073 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4074 \textcolor{comment}{SEE ALSO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075 \textcolor{comment}{    Spline1DFitCubicWC()    -\/   fitting by Cubic splines (less flexible,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076 \textcolor{comment}{                                more smooth)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4077 \textcolor{comment}{    Spline1DFitHermite()    -\/   "{}lightweight"{} Hermite fitting, without}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4078 \textcolor{comment}{                                invididual weights and constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4079 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4080 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4081 \textcolor{comment}{    X   -\/   points, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4082 \textcolor{comment}{    Y   -\/   function values, array[0..N-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4083 \textcolor{comment}{    W   -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4084 \textcolor{comment}{            Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation deviations from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4085 \textcolor{comment}{            given  values  is  multiplied  by  the square of corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4086 \textcolor{comment}{            weight. Fill it by 1's if you don't  want  to  solve  weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4087 \textcolor{comment}{            task.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4088 \textcolor{comment}{    N   -\/   number of points (optional):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4089 \textcolor{comment}{            * N>0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4090 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only first N elements of X/Y/W are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4091 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from X/Y/W sizes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4092 \textcolor{comment}{    XC  -\/   points where spline values/derivatives are constrained,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4093 \textcolor{comment}{            array[0..K-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4094 \textcolor{comment}{    YC  -\/   values of constraints, array[0..K-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4095 \textcolor{comment}{    DC  -\/   array[0..K-\/1], types of constraints:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4096 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=0   means that S(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4097 \textcolor{comment}{            * DC[i]=1   means that S'(XC[i])=YC[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4098 \textcolor{comment}{            SEE BELOW FOR IMPORTANT INFORMATION ON CONSTRAINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4099 \textcolor{comment}{    K   -\/   number of constraints (optional):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4100 \textcolor{comment}{            * 0<=K<M.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4101 \textcolor{comment}{            * K=0 means no constraints (XC/YC/DC are not used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4102 \textcolor{comment}{            * if given, only first K elements of XC/YC/DC are used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4103 \textcolor{comment}{            * if not given, automatically determined from XC/YC/DC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4104 \textcolor{comment}{    M   -\/   number of basis functions (= 2 * number of nodes),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4105 \textcolor{comment}{            M>=4,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4106 \textcolor{comment}{            M IS EVEN!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4107 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4108 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4109 \textcolor{comment}{    Info-\/   same format as in LSFitLinearW() subroutine:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4110 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info>0    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4111 \textcolor{comment}{            * Info<=0   an error occured:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4112 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/4 means inconvergence of internal SVD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4113 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/3 means inconsistent constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4114 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/2 means odd M was passed (which is not supported)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4115 \textcolor{comment}{                        -\/1 means another errors in parameters passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4116 \textcolor{comment}{                           (N<=0, for example)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4117 \textcolor{comment}{    S   -\/   spline interpolant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4118 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep -\/   report, same format as in LSFitLinearW() subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4119 \textcolor{comment}{            Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4120 \textcolor{comment}{            * RMSError      rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4121 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgError      average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4122 \textcolor{comment}{            * AvgRelError   average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4123 \textcolor{comment}{            * MaxError      maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4124 \textcolor{comment}{                            NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4125 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4126 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4127 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4128 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4129 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4130 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine supports only even M's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4131 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4132 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4133 \textcolor{comment}{ORDER OF POINTS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4134 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4135 \textcolor{comment}{Subroutine automatically sorts points, so caller may pass unsorted array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4136 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4137 \textcolor{comment}{SETTING CONSTRAINTS -\/ DANGERS AND OPPORTUNITIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4138 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4139 \textcolor{comment}{Setting constraints can lead  to undesired  results,  like ill-\/conditioned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4140 \textcolor{comment}{behavior, or inconsistency being detected. From the other side,  it allows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4141 \textcolor{comment}{us to improve quality of the fit. Here we summarize  our  experience  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4142 \textcolor{comment}{constrained regression splines:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4143 \textcolor{comment}{* excessive constraints can be inconsistent. Splines are  piecewise  cubic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4144 \textcolor{comment}{  functions, and it is easy to create an example, where  large  number  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4145 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints  concentrated  in  small  area will result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4146 \textcolor{comment}{  Just because spline is not flexible enough to satisfy all of  them.  And}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4147 \textcolor{comment}{  same constraints spread across the  [min(x),max(x)]  will  be  perfectly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4148 \textcolor{comment}{  consistent.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4149 \textcolor{comment}{* the more evenly constraints are spread across [min(x),max(x)],  the more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4150 \textcolor{comment}{  chances that they will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4151 \textcolor{comment}{* the  greater  is  M (given  fixed  constraints),  the  more chances that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4152 \textcolor{comment}{  constraints will be consistent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4153 \textcolor{comment}{* in the general case, consistency of constraints is NOT GUARANTEED.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4154 \textcolor{comment}{* in the several special cases, however, we can guarantee consistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4155 \textcolor{comment}{* one of this cases is  M>=4  and   constraints  on   the  function  value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4156 \textcolor{comment}{  (AND/OR its derivative) at the interval boundaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4157 \textcolor{comment}{* another special case is M>=4  and  ONE  constraint on the function value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4158 \textcolor{comment}{  (OR, BUT NOT AND, derivative) anywhere in [min(x),max(x)]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4159 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4160 \textcolor{comment}{Our final recommendation is to use constraints  WHEN  AND  ONLY  when  you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4161 \textcolor{comment}{can't solve your task without them. Anything beyond  special  cases  given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4162 \textcolor{comment}{above is not guaranteed and may result in inconsistency.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4163 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4164 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4271 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4272 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4273 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted linear least squares fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4274 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4275 \textcolor{comment}{QR decomposition is used to reduce task to MxM, then triangular solver  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4276 \textcolor{comment}{SVD-\/based solver is used depending on condition number of the  system.  It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4277 \textcolor{comment}{allows to maximize speed and retain decent accuracy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4278 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4279 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: if you want to perform  polynomial  fitting,  it  may  be  more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4280 \textcolor{comment}{           convenient to use PolynomialFit() function. This function gives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4281 \textcolor{comment}{           best  results  on  polynomial  problems  and  solves  numerical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4282 \textcolor{comment}{           stability  issues  which  arise  when   you   fit   high-\/degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4283 \textcolor{comment}{           polynomials to your data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4284 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4285 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4286 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1] Function values in  N  points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4287 \textcolor{comment}{    W       -\/   array[0..N-\/1]  Weights  corresponding to function  values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4288 \textcolor{comment}{                Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation  deviations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4289 \textcolor{comment}{                from  given  values  is  multiplied  by  the   square   of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4290 \textcolor{comment}{                corresponding weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4291 \textcolor{comment}{    FMatrix -\/   a table of basis functions values, array[0..N-\/1, 0..M-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4292 \textcolor{comment}{                FMatrix[I, J] -\/ value of J-\/th basis function in I-\/th point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4293 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points used. N>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4294 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   number of basis functions, M>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4295 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4296 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4297 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   error code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4298 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/4    internal SVD decomposition subroutine failed (very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4299 \textcolor{comment}{                        rare and for degenerate systems only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4300 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/1    incorrect N/M were specified}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4301 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4302 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   decomposition coefficients, array[0..M-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4303 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4304 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.TaskRCond     reciprocal of condition number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4305 \textcolor{comment}{                * R2                non-\/adjusted coefficient of determination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4306 \textcolor{comment}{                                    (non-\/weighted)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4307 \textcolor{comment}{                * RMSError          rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4308 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgError          average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4309 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgRelError       average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4310 \textcolor{comment}{                * MaxError          maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4311 \textcolor{comment}{                                    NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4312 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4313 \textcolor{comment}{ERRORS IN PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4314 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4315 \textcolor{comment}{This  solver  also  calculates different kinds of errors in parameters and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4316 \textcolor{comment}{fills corresponding fields of report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4317 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.CovPar        covariance matrix for parameters, array[K,K].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4318 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrPar        errors in parameters, array[K],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4319 \textcolor{comment}{                    errpar = sqrt(diag(CovPar))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4320 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrCurve      vector of fit errors -\/ standard deviations of empirical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4321 \textcolor{comment}{                    best-\/fit curve from "{}ideal"{} best-\/fit curve built  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4322 \textcolor{comment}{                    infinite number of samples, array[N].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4323 \textcolor{comment}{                    errcurve = sqrt(diag(F*CovPar*F')),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4324 \textcolor{comment}{                    where F is functions matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4325 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.Noise         vector of per-\/point estimates of noise, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4326 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4327 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       noise in the data is estimated as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4328 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting without user-\/supplied  weights  all  points  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4329 \textcolor{comment}{              assumed to have same level of noise, which is estimated from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4330 \textcolor{comment}{              the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4331 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting with user-\/supplied weights we assume that  noise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4332 \textcolor{comment}{              level in I-\/th point is inversely proportional to Ith weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4333 \textcolor{comment}{              Coefficient of proportionality is estimated from the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4334 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4335 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       we apply small amount of regularization when we invert squared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4336 \textcolor{comment}{            Jacobian and calculate covariance matrix. It  guarantees  that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4337 \textcolor{comment}{            algorithm won't divide by zero  during  inversion,  but  skews}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4338 \textcolor{comment}{            error estimates a bit (fractional error is about 10\string^-\/9).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4339 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4340 \textcolor{comment}{            However, we believe that this difference is insignificant  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4341 \textcolor{comment}{            all practical purposes except for the situation when you  want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4342 \textcolor{comment}{            to compare ALGLIB results with "{}reference"{}  implementation  up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4343 \textcolor{comment}{            to the last significant digit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4344 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4345 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       covariance matrix is estimated using  correction  for  degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4346 \textcolor{comment}{            of freedom (covariances are divided by N-\/M instead of dividing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4347 \textcolor{comment}{            by N).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4348 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4349 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4350 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4351 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4352 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4353 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4354 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4355 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4356 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We  recommend  you  to  read  'Compiling ALGLIB' section of the ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4357 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4358 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4359 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4360 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4361 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4362 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4363 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4364 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4365 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4366 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * hardware vendor (Intel) implementations of linear algebra primitives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4367 \textcolor{comment}{  !   (C++ and C\# versions, x86/x64 platform)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4368 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4369 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We recommend you to read 'Working with commercial version' section  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4370 \textcolor{comment}{  ! ALGLIB Reference Manual in order to find out how to  use  performance-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4371 \textcolor{comment}{  ! related features provided by commercial edition of ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4372 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4373 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4374 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 17.08.2009 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4375 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4376 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} lsfitlinearw(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&fmatrix, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&c, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4377 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} lsfitlinearw(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&w, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&fmatrix, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&c, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4379 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4380 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4381 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted constained linear least squares fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4382 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4383 \textcolor{comment}{This  is  variation  of LSFitLinearW(), which searchs for min|A*x=b| given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4384 \textcolor{comment}{that  K  additional  constaints  C*x=bc are satisfied. It reduces original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4385 \textcolor{comment}{task to modified one: min|B*y-\/d| WITHOUT constraints,  then LSFitLinearW()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4386 \textcolor{comment}{is called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4387 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4388 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: if you want to perform  polynomial  fitting,  it  may  be  more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4389 \textcolor{comment}{           convenient to use PolynomialFit() function. This function gives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4390 \textcolor{comment}{           best  results  on  polynomial  problems  and  solves  numerical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4391 \textcolor{comment}{           stability  issues  which  arise  when   you   fit   high-\/degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4392 \textcolor{comment}{           polynomials to your data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4393 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4394 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4395 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1] Function values in  N  points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4396 \textcolor{comment}{    W       -\/   array[0..N-\/1]  Weights  corresponding to function  values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4397 \textcolor{comment}{                Each summand in square  sum  of  approximation  deviations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4398 \textcolor{comment}{                from  given  values  is  multiplied  by  the   square   of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4399 \textcolor{comment}{                corresponding weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4400 \textcolor{comment}{    FMatrix -\/   a table of basis functions values, array[0..N-\/1, 0..M-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4401 \textcolor{comment}{                FMatrix[I,J] -\/ value of J-\/th basis function in I-\/th point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4402 \textcolor{comment}{    CMatrix -\/   a table of constaints, array[0..K-\/1,0..M].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4403 \textcolor{comment}{                I-\/th row of CMatrix corresponds to I-\/th linear constraint:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4404 \textcolor{comment}{                CMatrix[I,0]*C[0] + ... + CMatrix[I,M-\/1]*C[M-\/1] = CMatrix[I,M]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4405 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points used. N>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4406 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   number of basis functions, M>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4407 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   number of constraints, 0 <= K < M}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408 \textcolor{comment}{                K=0 corresponds to absence of constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4409 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4410 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4411 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   error code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4412 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/4    internal SVD decomposition subroutine failed (very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4413 \textcolor{comment}{                        rare and for degenerate systems only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    either   too   many  constraints  (M   or   more),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4415 \textcolor{comment}{                        degenerate  constraints   (some   constraints  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416 \textcolor{comment}{                        repetead twice) or inconsistent  constraints  were}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4417 \textcolor{comment}{                        specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4418 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4419 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   decomposition coefficients, array[0..M-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4420 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4421 \textcolor{comment}{                * R2                non-\/adjusted coefficient of determination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4422 \textcolor{comment}{                                    (non-\/weighted)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423 \textcolor{comment}{                * RMSError          rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4424 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgError          average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4425 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgRelError       average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4426 \textcolor{comment}{                * MaxError          maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4427 \textcolor{comment}{                                    NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4428 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4429 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4430 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4432 \textcolor{comment}{ERRORS IN PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4434 \textcolor{comment}{This  solver  also  calculates different kinds of errors in parameters and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435 \textcolor{comment}{fills corresponding fields of report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4436 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.CovPar        covariance matrix for parameters, array[K,K].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrPar        errors in parameters, array[K],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438 \textcolor{comment}{                    errpar = sqrt(diag(CovPar))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrCurve      vector of fit errors -\/ standard deviations of empirical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4440 \textcolor{comment}{                    best-\/fit curve from "{}ideal"{} best-\/fit curve built  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441 \textcolor{comment}{                    infinite number of samples, array[N].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 \textcolor{comment}{                    errcurve = sqrt(diag(F*CovPar*F')),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4443 \textcolor{comment}{                    where F is functions matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.Noise         vector of per-\/point estimates of noise, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:  errors  in  parameters  are  calculated  without  taking  into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447 \textcolor{comment}{            account boundary/linear constraints! Presence  of  constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448 \textcolor{comment}{            changes distribution of errors, but there is no  easy  way  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4449 \textcolor{comment}{            account for constraints when you calculate covariance matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4450 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4451 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       noise in the data is estimated as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4452 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting without user-\/supplied  weights  all  points  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4453 \textcolor{comment}{              assumed to have same level of noise, which is estimated from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4454 \textcolor{comment}{              the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4455 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting with user-\/supplied weights we assume that  noise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456 \textcolor{comment}{              level in I-\/th point is inversely proportional to Ith weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4457 \textcolor{comment}{              Coefficient of proportionality is estimated from the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4458 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       we apply small amount of regularization when we invert squared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4460 \textcolor{comment}{            Jacobian and calculate covariance matrix. It  guarantees  that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4461 \textcolor{comment}{            algorithm won't divide by zero  during  inversion,  but  skews}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462 \textcolor{comment}{            error estimates a bit (fractional error is about 10\string^-\/9).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4463 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4464 \textcolor{comment}{            However, we believe that this difference is insignificant  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4465 \textcolor{comment}{            all practical purposes except for the situation when you  want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466 \textcolor{comment}{            to compare ALGLIB results with "{}reference"{}  implementation  up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4467 \textcolor{comment}{            to the last significant digit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4468 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4469 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       covariance matrix is estimated using  correction  for  degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4470 \textcolor{comment}{            of freedom (covariances are divided by N-\/M instead of dividing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4471 \textcolor{comment}{            by N).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4472 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4473 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4474 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4478 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4503 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4504 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4505 \textcolor{comment}{Linear least squares fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4506 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4507 \textcolor{comment}{QR decomposition is used to reduce task to MxM, then triangular solver  or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4508 \textcolor{comment}{SVD-\/based solver is used depending on condition number of the  system.  It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4509 \textcolor{comment}{allows to maximize speed and retain decent accuracy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4510 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4511 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: if you want to perform  polynomial  fitting,  it  may  be  more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4512 \textcolor{comment}{           convenient to use PolynomialFit() function. This function gives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4513 \textcolor{comment}{           best  results  on  polynomial  problems  and  solves  numerical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4514 \textcolor{comment}{           stability  issues  which  arise  when   you   fit   high-\/degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4515 \textcolor{comment}{           polynomials to your data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4516 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4517 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4518 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1] Function values in  N  points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4519 \textcolor{comment}{    FMatrix -\/   a table of basis functions values, array[0..N-\/1, 0..M-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4520 \textcolor{comment}{                FMatrix[I, J] -\/ value of J-\/th basis function in I-\/th point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4521 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points used. N>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4522 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   number of basis functions, M>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4523 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4524 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4525 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   error code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4526 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/4    internal SVD decomposition subroutine failed (very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4527 \textcolor{comment}{                        rare and for degenerate systems only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4528 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4529 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   decomposition coefficients, array[0..M-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4530 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4531 \textcolor{comment}{                * Rep.TaskRCond     reciprocal of condition number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4532 \textcolor{comment}{                * R2                non-\/adjusted coefficient of determination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4533 \textcolor{comment}{                                    (non-\/weighted)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4534 \textcolor{comment}{                * RMSError          rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4535 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgError          average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4536 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgRelError       average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4537 \textcolor{comment}{                * MaxError          maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4538 \textcolor{comment}{                                    NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4539 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4540 \textcolor{comment}{ERRORS IN PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4541 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4542 \textcolor{comment}{This  solver  also  calculates different kinds of errors in parameters and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4543 \textcolor{comment}{fills corresponding fields of report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4544 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.CovPar        covariance matrix for parameters, array[K,K].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4545 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrPar        errors in parameters, array[K],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4546 \textcolor{comment}{                    errpar = sqrt(diag(CovPar))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4547 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrCurve      vector of fit errors -\/ standard deviations of empirical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4548 \textcolor{comment}{                    best-\/fit curve from "{}ideal"{} best-\/fit curve built  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4549 \textcolor{comment}{                    infinite number of samples, array[N].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4550 \textcolor{comment}{                    errcurve = sqrt(diag(F*CovPar*F')),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4551 \textcolor{comment}{                    where F is functions matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4552 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.Noise         vector of per-\/point estimates of noise, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4553 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4554 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       noise in the data is estimated as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4555 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting without user-\/supplied  weights  all  points  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4556 \textcolor{comment}{              assumed to have same level of noise, which is estimated from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4557 \textcolor{comment}{              the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4558 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting with user-\/supplied weights we assume that  noise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4559 \textcolor{comment}{              level in I-\/th point is inversely proportional to Ith weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4560 \textcolor{comment}{              Coefficient of proportionality is estimated from the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4561 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4562 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       we apply small amount of regularization when we invert squared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4563 \textcolor{comment}{            Jacobian and calculate covariance matrix. It  guarantees  that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564 \textcolor{comment}{            algorithm won't divide by zero  during  inversion,  but  skews}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4565 \textcolor{comment}{            error estimates a bit (fractional error is about 10\string^-\/9).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4566 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4567 \textcolor{comment}{            However, we believe that this difference is insignificant  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4568 \textcolor{comment}{            all practical purposes except for the situation when you  want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4569 \textcolor{comment}{            to compare ALGLIB results with "{}reference"{}  implementation  up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4570 \textcolor{comment}{            to the last significant digit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4571 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4572 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       covariance matrix is estimated using  correction  for  degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4573 \textcolor{comment}{            of freedom (covariances are divided by N-\/M instead of dividing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4574 \textcolor{comment}{            by N).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4575 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4576 \textcolor{comment}{  ! FREE EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4577 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4578 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Free Edition of ALGLIB supports following important features for  this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4579 \textcolor{comment}{  ! function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4580 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C++ version: x64 SIMD support using C++ intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4581 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * C\#  version: x64 SIMD support using NET5/NetCore hardware intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4582 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4584 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Reference Manual in order  to  find  out  how to activate SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4585 \textcolor{comment}{  ! in ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4586 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4603 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} lsfitlinear(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&fmatrix, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t m, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&c, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4604 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} lsfitlinear(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{real\_2d\_array}} \&fmatrix, ae\_int\_t \&info, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&c, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1lsfitreport}{lsfitreport}} \&rep, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4606 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4607 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4608 \textcolor{comment}{Constained linear least squares fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4609 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4610 \textcolor{comment}{This  is  variation  of LSFitLinear(),  which searchs for min|A*x=b| given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4611 \textcolor{comment}{that  K  additional  constaints  C*x=bc are satisfied. It reduces original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4612 \textcolor{comment}{task to modified one: min|B*y-\/d| WITHOUT constraints,  then  LSFitLinear()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4613 \textcolor{comment}{is called.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4614 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4615 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: if you want to perform  polynomial  fitting,  it  may  be  more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4616 \textcolor{comment}{           convenient to use PolynomialFit() function. This function gives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4617 \textcolor{comment}{           best  results  on  polynomial  problems  and  solves  numerical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4618 \textcolor{comment}{           stability  issues  which  arise  when   you   fit   high-\/degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4619 \textcolor{comment}{           polynomials to your data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4620 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4621 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4622 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1] Function values in  N  points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4623 \textcolor{comment}{    FMatrix -\/   a table of basis functions values, array[0..N-\/1, 0..M-\/1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4624 \textcolor{comment}{                FMatrix[I,J] -\/ value of J-\/th basis function in I-\/th point.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4625 \textcolor{comment}{    CMatrix -\/   a table of constaints, array[0..K-\/1,0..M].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4626 \textcolor{comment}{                I-\/th row of CMatrix corresponds to I-\/th linear constraint:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4627 \textcolor{comment}{                CMatrix[I,0]*C[0] + ... + CMatrix[I,M-\/1]*C[M-\/1] = CMatrix[I,M]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4628 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points used. N>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4629 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   number of basis functions, M>=1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4630 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   number of constraints, 0 <= K < M}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4631 \textcolor{comment}{                K=0 corresponds to absence of constraints.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4632 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4633 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4634 \textcolor{comment}{    Info    -\/   error code:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4635 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/4    internal SVD decomposition subroutine failed (very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4636 \textcolor{comment}{                        rare and for degenerate systems only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4637 \textcolor{comment}{                * -\/3    either   too   many  constraints  (M   or   more),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4638 \textcolor{comment}{                        degenerate  constraints   (some   constraints  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4639 \textcolor{comment}{                        repetead twice) or inconsistent  constraints  were}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4640 \textcolor{comment}{                        specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4641 \textcolor{comment}{                *  1    task is solved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4642 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   decomposition coefficients, array[0..M-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4643 \textcolor{comment}{    Rep     -\/   fitting report. Following fields are set:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4644 \textcolor{comment}{                * R2                non-\/adjusted coefficient of determination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4645 \textcolor{comment}{                                    (non-\/weighted)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4646 \textcolor{comment}{                * RMSError          rms error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4647 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgError          average error on the (X,Y).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4648 \textcolor{comment}{                * AvgRelError       average relative error on the non-\/zero Y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4649 \textcolor{comment}{                * MaxError          maximum error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4650 \textcolor{comment}{                                    NON-\/WEIGHTED ERRORS ARE CALCULATED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4651 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4652 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4653 \textcolor{comment}{    this subroitine doesn't calculate task's condition number for K<>0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4654 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4655 \textcolor{comment}{ERRORS IN PARAMETERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4656 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4657 \textcolor{comment}{This  solver  also  calculates different kinds of errors in parameters and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4658 \textcolor{comment}{fills corresponding fields of report:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4659 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.CovPar        covariance matrix for parameters, array[K,K].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4660 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrPar        errors in parameters, array[K],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4661 \textcolor{comment}{                    errpar = sqrt(diag(CovPar))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4662 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.ErrCurve      vector of fit errors -\/ standard deviations of empirical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4663 \textcolor{comment}{                    best-\/fit curve from "{}ideal"{} best-\/fit curve built  with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4664 \textcolor{comment}{                    infinite number of samples, array[N].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4665 \textcolor{comment}{                    errcurve = sqrt(diag(F*CovPar*F')),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4666 \textcolor{comment}{                    where F is functions matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4667 \textcolor{comment}{* Rep.Noise         vector of per-\/point estimates of noise, array[N]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4668 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4669 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT:  errors  in  parameters  are  calculated  without  taking  into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4670 \textcolor{comment}{            account boundary/linear constraints! Presence  of  constraints}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4671 \textcolor{comment}{            changes distribution of errors, but there is no  easy  way  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4672 \textcolor{comment}{            account for constraints when you calculate covariance matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4673 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4674 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       noise in the data is estimated as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4675 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting without user-\/supplied  weights  all  points  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4676 \textcolor{comment}{              assumed to have same level of noise, which is estimated from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4677 \textcolor{comment}{              the data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4678 \textcolor{comment}{            * for fitting with user-\/supplied weights we assume that  noise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4679 \textcolor{comment}{              level in I-\/th point is inversely proportional to Ith weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4680 \textcolor{comment}{              Coefficient of proportionality is estimated from the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4681 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4682 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       we apply small amount of regularization when we invert squared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4683 \textcolor{comment}{            Jacobian and calculate covariance matrix. It  guarantees  that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4684 \textcolor{comment}{            algorithm won't divide by zero  during  inversion,  but  skews}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4685 \textcolor{comment}{            error estimates a bit (fractional error is about 10\string^-\/9).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4686 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4687 \textcolor{comment}{            However, we believe that this difference is insignificant  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4688 \textcolor{comment}{            all practical purposes except for the situation when you  want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4689 \textcolor{comment}{            to compare ALGLIB results with "{}reference"{}  implementation  up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4690 \textcolor{comment}{            to the last significant digit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4691 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4692 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE:       covariance matrix is estimated using  correction  for  degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4693 \textcolor{comment}{            of freedom (covariances are divided by N-\/M instead of dividing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4694 \textcolor{comment}{            by N).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4695 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4697 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4727 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted nonlinear least squares fitting using function values only.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730 \textcolor{comment}{Combination of numerical differentiation and secant updates is used to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731 \textcolor{comment}{obtain function Jacobian.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4732 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4733 \textcolor{comment}{Nonlinear task min(F(c)) is solved, where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4734 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4735 \textcolor{comment}{    F(c) = (w[0]*(f(c,x[0])-\/y[0]))\string^2 + ... + (w[n-\/1]*(f(c,x[n-\/1])-\/y[n-\/1]))\string^2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737 \textcolor{comment}{    * N is a number of points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 \textcolor{comment}{    * M is a dimension of a space points belong to,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4739 \textcolor{comment}{    * K is a dimension of a space of parameters being fitted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740 \textcolor{comment}{    * w is an N-\/dimensional vector of weight coefficients,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741 \textcolor{comment}{    * x is a set of N points, each of them is an M-\/dimensional vector,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742 \textcolor{comment}{    * c is a K-\/dimensional vector of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine uses only f(c,x[i]).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4746 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], points (one row = one point)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], function values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4749 \textcolor{comment}{    W       -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4750 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   array[0..K-\/1], initial approximation to the solution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points, N>1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   dimension of space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   number of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4754 \textcolor{comment}{    DiffStep-\/   numerical differentiation step;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4755 \textcolor{comment}{                should not be very small or large;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4756 \textcolor{comment}{                large = loss of accuracy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4757 \textcolor{comment}{                small = growth of round-\/off errors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4758 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4759 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4760 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4761 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4762 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4763 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 18.10.2008 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4764 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4810 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4811 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted nonlinear least squares fitting using gradient only.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4812 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4813 \textcolor{comment}{Nonlinear task min(F(c)) is solved, where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4814 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4815 \textcolor{comment}{    F(c) = (w[0]*(f(c,x[0])-\/y[0]))\string^2 + ... + (w[n-\/1]*(f(c,x[n-\/1])-\/y[n-\/1]))\string^2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4816 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4817 \textcolor{comment}{    * N is a number of points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4818 \textcolor{comment}{    * M is a dimension of a space points belong to,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4819 \textcolor{comment}{    * K is a dimension of a space of parameters being fitted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4820 \textcolor{comment}{    * w is an N-\/dimensional vector of weight coefficients,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4821 \textcolor{comment}{    * x is a set of N points, each of them is an M-\/dimensional vector,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4822 \textcolor{comment}{    * c is a K-\/dimensional vector of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4823 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4824 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine uses only f(c,x[i]) and its gradient.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4825 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4826 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4827 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], points (one row = one point)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4829 \textcolor{comment}{    W       -\/   weights, array[0..N-\/1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4830 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   array[0..K-\/1], initial approximation to the solution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4831 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points, N>1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4832 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   dimension of space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4833 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   number of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4834 \textcolor{comment}{    CheapFG -\/   boolean flag, which is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4835 \textcolor{comment}{                * True  if both function and gradient calculation complexity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4836 \textcolor{comment}{                        are less than O(M\string^2).  An improved  algorithm  can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4837 \textcolor{comment}{                        be  used  which corresponds  to  FGJ  scheme  from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4838 \textcolor{comment}{                        MINLM unit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4839 \textcolor{comment}{                * False otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4840 \textcolor{comment}{                        Standard Jacibian-\/bases  Levenberg-\/Marquardt  algo}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4841 \textcolor{comment}{                        will be used (FJ scheme).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4842 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4902 \textcolor{comment}{Weighted nonlinear least squares fitting using gradient/Hessian.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4903 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4904 \textcolor{comment}{Nonlinear task min(F(c)) is solved, where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4905 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4906 \textcolor{comment}{    F(c) = (w[0]*(f(c,x[0])-\/y[0]))\string^2 + ... + (w[n-\/1]*(f(c,x[n-\/1])-\/y[n-\/1]))\string^2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4907 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4908 \textcolor{comment}{    * N is a number of points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4909 \textcolor{comment}{    * M is a dimension of a space points belong to,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4910 \textcolor{comment}{    * K is a dimension of a space of parameters being fitted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4911 \textcolor{comment}{    * w is an N-\/dimensional vector of weight coefficients,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4912 \textcolor{comment}{    * x is a set of N points, each of them is an M-\/dimensional vector,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4913 \textcolor{comment}{    * c is a K-\/dimensional vector of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4914 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4915 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine uses f(c,x[i]), its gradient and its Hessian.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4936 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4937 \textcolor{comment}{Nonlinear least squares fitting using gradient/Hessian, without individial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4938 \textcolor{comment}{weights.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4939 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4940 \textcolor{comment}{Nonlinear task min(F(c)) is solved, where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4941 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4942 \textcolor{comment}{    F(c) = ((f(c,x[0])-\/y[0]))\string^2 + ... + ((f(c,x[n-\/1])-\/y[n-\/1]))\string^2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4943 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4944 \textcolor{comment}{    * N is a number of points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4945 \textcolor{comment}{    * M is a dimension of a space points belong to,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4946 \textcolor{comment}{    * K is a dimension of a space of parameters being fitted,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4947 \textcolor{comment}{    * x is a set of N points, each of them is an M-\/dimensional vector,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4948 \textcolor{comment}{    * c is a K-\/dimensional vector of parameters being fitted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4949 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4950 \textcolor{comment}{This subroutine uses f(c,x[i]), its gradient and its Hessian.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4951 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4952 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4953 \textcolor{comment}{    X       -\/   array[0..N-\/1,0..M-\/1], points (one row = one point)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4954 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   array[0..N-\/1], function values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4955 \textcolor{comment}{    C       -\/   array[0..K-\/1], initial approximation to the solution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4956 \textcolor{comment}{    N       -\/   number of points, N>1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4957 \textcolor{comment}{    M       -\/   dimension of space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4958 \textcolor{comment}{    K       -\/   number of parameters being fitted}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4971 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4972 \textcolor{comment}{Stopping conditions for nonlinear least squares fitting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4973 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4974 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4975 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4976 \textcolor{comment}{    EpsX    -\/   >=0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4977 \textcolor{comment}{                The subroutine finishes its work if  on  k+1-\/th  iteration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4978 \textcolor{comment}{                the condition |v|<=EpsX is fulfilled, where:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4979 \textcolor{comment}{                * |.| means Euclidian norm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4980 \textcolor{comment}{                * v -\/ scaled step vector, v[i]=dx[i]/s[i]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4981 \textcolor{comment}{                * dx -\/ ste pvector, dx=X(k+1)-\/X(k)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4982 \textcolor{comment}{                * s -\/ scaling coefficients set by LSFitSetScale()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4983 \textcolor{comment}{    MaxIts  -\/   maximum number of iterations. If MaxIts=0, the  number  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4984 \textcolor{comment}{                iterations   is    unlimited.   Only   Levenberg-\/Marquardt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4985 \textcolor{comment}{                iterations  are  counted  (L-\/BFGS/CG  iterations  are  NOT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4986 \textcolor{comment}{                counted because their cost is very low compared to that of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4987 \textcolor{comment}{                LM).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4988 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4989 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4990 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4991 \textcolor{comment}{Passing EpsX=0  and  MaxIts=0  (simultaneously)  will  lead  to  automatic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4992 \textcolor{comment}{stopping criterion selection (according to the scheme used by MINLM unit).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4993 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4994 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4995 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4996 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 17.08.2009 by Bochkanov Sergey}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5001 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5002 \textcolor{comment}{This function sets maximum step length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5003 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5004 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5005 \textcolor{comment}{    State   -\/   structure which stores algorithm state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5006 \textcolor{comment}{    StpMax  -\/   maximum step length, >=0. Set StpMax to 0.0,  if you don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5007 \textcolor{comment}{                want to limit step length.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5008 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5009 \textcolor{comment}{Use this subroutine when you optimize target function which contains exp()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5010 \textcolor{comment}{or  other  fast  growing  functions,  and optimization algorithm makes too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5011 \textcolor{comment}{large  steps  which  leads  to overflow. This function allows us to reject}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5012 \textcolor{comment}{steps  that  are  too  large  (and  therefore  expose  us  to the possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5013 \textcolor{comment}{overflow) without actually calculating function value at the x+stp*d.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5014 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5015 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: non-\/zero StpMax leads to moderate  performance  degradation  because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5016 \textcolor{comment}{intermediate  step  of  preconditioned L-\/BFGS optimization is incompatible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5017 \textcolor{comment}{with limits on step size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5018 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5019 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5020 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 02.04.2010 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5021 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
