\DoxyCodeLine{8074 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8075 \textcolor{comment}{This function calculates values of the RBF  model  at  the  regular  grid,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8076 \textcolor{comment}{which  has  N0*N1 points, with Point[I,J] = (X0[I], X1[J]).  Vector-\/valued}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8077 \textcolor{comment}{RBF models are supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8078 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8079 \textcolor{comment}{This function returns 0.0 when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8080 \textcolor{comment}{* model is not initialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8081 \textcolor{comment}{* NX<>2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8082 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8083 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8084 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8085 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8086 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8087 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8088 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8089 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8090 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We recommend you to read 'Working with commercial version' section  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8091 \textcolor{comment}{  ! ALGLIB Reference Manual in order to find out how to  use  performance-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8092 \textcolor{comment}{  ! related features provided by commercial edition of ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8093 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8094 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: Parallel  processing  is  implemented only for modern (hierarchical)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8095 \textcolor{comment}{      RBFs. Legacy version 1 RBFs (created  by  QNN  or  RBF-\/ML) are still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8096 \textcolor{comment}{      processed serially.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8097 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8098 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8099 \textcolor{comment}{    S       -\/   RBF model, used in read-\/only mode, can be  shared  between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8100 \textcolor{comment}{                multiple   invocations  of  this  function  from  multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8101 \textcolor{comment}{                threads.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8102 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8103 \textcolor{comment}{    X0      -\/   array of grid nodes, first coordinates, array[N0].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8104 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8105 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8106 \textcolor{comment}{    N0      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the first dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8107 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8108 \textcolor{comment}{    X1      -\/   array of grid nodes, second coordinates, array[N1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8109 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8110 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8111 \textcolor{comment}{    N1      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the second dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8112 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8113 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8114 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   function values, array[NY*N0*N1], where NY is a  number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8115 \textcolor{comment}{                "{}output"{} vector values (this  function   supports  vector-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8116 \textcolor{comment}{                valued RBF models). Y is out-\/variable and  is  reallocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8117 \textcolor{comment}{                by this function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8118 \textcolor{comment}{                Y[K+NY*(I0+I1*N0)]=F\_k(X0[I0],X1[I1]), for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8119 \textcolor{comment}{                *  K=0...NY-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8120 \textcolor{comment}{                * I0=0...N0-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8121 \textcolor{comment}{                * I1=0...N1-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8122 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8123 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function supports weakly ordered grid nodes, i.e. you may  have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8124 \textcolor{comment}{      X[i]=X[i+1] for some i. It does  not  provide  you  any  performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8125 \textcolor{comment}{      benefits  due  to   duplication  of  points,  just  convenience  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8126 \textcolor{comment}{      flexibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8127 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8128 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this  function  is  re-\/entrant,  i.e.  you  may  use  same  rbfmodel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8129 \textcolor{comment}{      structure in multiple threads calling  this function  for  different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8130 \textcolor{comment}{      grids.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8131 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8132 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need function values on some subset  of  regular  grid, which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8133 \textcolor{comment}{      may be described as "{}several compact and  dense  islands"{},  you  may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8134 \textcolor{comment}{      use rbfgridcalc2vsubset().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8135 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8136 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8137 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 27.01.2017 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8138 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8139 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} rbfgridcalc2v(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1rbfmodel}{rbfmodel}} \&s, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x0, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n0, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&x1, \textcolor{keyword}{const} ae\_int\_t n1, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__1d__array}{real\_1d\_array}} \&y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib_1_1xparams}{xparams}} \_xparams = alglib::xdefault);}

\DoxyCodeLine{8142 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8143 \textcolor{comment}{This function calculates values of the RBF model at some subset of regular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8144 \textcolor{comment}{grid:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8145 \textcolor{comment}{* grid has N0*N1 points, with Point[I,J] = (X0[I], X1[J])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8146 \textcolor{comment}{* only values at some subset of this grid are required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8147 \textcolor{comment}{Vector-\/valued RBF models are supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8148 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8149 \textcolor{comment}{This function returns 0.0 when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8150 \textcolor{comment}{* model is not initialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8151 \textcolor{comment}{* NX<>2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8152 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8153 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8154 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8155 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8156 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8157 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8158 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8159 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8160 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We recommend you to read 'Working with commercial version' section  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8161 \textcolor{comment}{  ! ALGLIB Reference Manual in order to find out how to  use  performance-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8162 \textcolor{comment}{  ! related features provided by commercial edition of ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8163 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8164 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: Parallel  processing  is  implemented only for modern (hierarchical)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8165 \textcolor{comment}{      RBFs. Legacy version 1 RBFs (created  by  QNN  or  RBF-\/ML) are still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8166 \textcolor{comment}{      processed serially.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8167 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8168 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8169 \textcolor{comment}{    S       -\/   RBF model, used in read-\/only mode, can be  shared  between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8170 \textcolor{comment}{                multiple   invocations  of  this  function  from  multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8171 \textcolor{comment}{                threads.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8172 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8173 \textcolor{comment}{    X0      -\/   array of grid nodes, first coordinates, array[N0].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8174 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8175 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8176 \textcolor{comment}{    N0      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the first dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8177 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8178 \textcolor{comment}{    X1      -\/   array of grid nodes, second coordinates, array[N1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8179 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8180 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8181 \textcolor{comment}{    N1      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the second dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8182 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8183 \textcolor{comment}{    FlagY   -\/   array[N0*N1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8184 \textcolor{comment}{                * Y[I0+I1*N0] corresponds to node (X0[I0],X1[I1])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8185 \textcolor{comment}{                * it is a "{}bitmap"{} array which contains  False  for  nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8186 \textcolor{comment}{                  which are NOT calculated, and True for nodes  which  are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8187 \textcolor{comment}{                  required.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8188 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8189 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8190 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   function values, array[NY*N0*N1*N2], where NY is a  number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8191 \textcolor{comment}{                of "{}output"{} vector values (this function  supports vector-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8192 \textcolor{comment}{                valued RBF models):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8193 \textcolor{comment}{                * Y[K+NY*(I0+I1*N0)]=F\_k(X0[I0],X1[I1]),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8194 \textcolor{comment}{                  for K=0...NY-\/1, I0=0...N0-\/1, I1=0...N1-\/1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8195 \textcolor{comment}{                * elements of Y[] which correspond  to  FlagY[]=True   are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8196 \textcolor{comment}{                  loaded by model values (which may be  exactly  zero  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8197 \textcolor{comment}{                  some nodes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8198 \textcolor{comment}{                * elements of Y[] which correspond to FlagY[]=False MAY be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8199 \textcolor{comment}{                  initialized by zeros OR may be calculated. This function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8200 \textcolor{comment}{                  processes  grid  as  a  hierarchy  of  nested blocks and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8201 \textcolor{comment}{                  micro-\/rows. If just one element of micro-\/row is required,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8202 \textcolor{comment}{                  entire micro-\/row (up to 8 nodes in the current  version,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8203 \textcolor{comment}{                  but no promises) is calculated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8204 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8205 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function supports weakly ordered grid nodes, i.e. you may  have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8206 \textcolor{comment}{      X[i]=X[i+1] for some i. It does  not  provide  you  any  performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8207 \textcolor{comment}{      benefits  due  to   duplication  of  points,  just  convenience  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8208 \textcolor{comment}{      flexibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8209 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8210 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this  function  is  re-\/entrant,  i.e.  you  may  use  same  rbfmodel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8211 \textcolor{comment}{      structure in multiple threads calling  this function  for  different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8212 \textcolor{comment}{      grids.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8213 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8214 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8220 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8221 \textcolor{comment}{This function calculates values of the RBF  model  at  the  regular  grid,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8222 \textcolor{comment}{which  has  N0*N1*N2  points,  with  Point[I,J,K] = (X0[I], X1[J], X2[K]).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8223 \textcolor{comment}{Vector-\/valued RBF models are supported.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8224 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8225 \textcolor{comment}{This function returns 0.0 when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8226 \textcolor{comment}{* model is not initialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8227 \textcolor{comment}{* NX<>3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8228 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8229 \textcolor{comment}{  ! COMMERCIAL EDITION OF ALGLIB:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8230 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8231 \textcolor{comment}{  ! Commercial Edition of ALGLIB includes following important improvements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8232 \textcolor{comment}{  ! of this function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8233 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * high-\/performance native backend with same C\# interface (C\# version)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8234 \textcolor{comment}{  ! * multithreading support (C++ and C\# versions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8235 \textcolor{comment}{  !}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8236 \textcolor{comment}{  ! We recommend you to read 'Working with commercial version' section  of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8237 \textcolor{comment}{  ! ALGLIB Reference Manual in order to find out how to  use  performance-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8238 \textcolor{comment}{  ! related features provided by commercial edition of ALGLIB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8239 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8240 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: Parallel  processing  is  implemented only for modern (hierarchical)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8241 \textcolor{comment}{      RBFs. Legacy version 1 RBFs (created  by  QNN  or  RBF-\/ML) are still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8242 \textcolor{comment}{      processed serially.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8243 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8244 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8245 \textcolor{comment}{    S       -\/   RBF model, used in read-\/only mode, can be  shared  between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8246 \textcolor{comment}{                multiple   invocations  of  this  function  from  multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8247 \textcolor{comment}{                threads.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8248 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8249 \textcolor{comment}{    X0      -\/   array of grid nodes, first coordinates, array[N0].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8250 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8251 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8252 \textcolor{comment}{    N0      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the first dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8253 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8254 \textcolor{comment}{    X1      -\/   array of grid nodes, second coordinates, array[N1]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8255 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8256 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8257 \textcolor{comment}{    N1      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the second dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8258 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8259 \textcolor{comment}{    X2      -\/   array of grid nodes, third coordinates, array[N2]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8260 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8261 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8262 \textcolor{comment}{    N2      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the third dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8263 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8264 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8265 \textcolor{comment}{    Y       -\/   function values, array[NY*N0*N1*N2], where NY is a  number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8266 \textcolor{comment}{                of "{}output"{} vector values (this function  supports vector-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8267 \textcolor{comment}{                valued RBF models). Y is out-\/variable and  is  reallocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8268 \textcolor{comment}{                by this function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8269 \textcolor{comment}{                Y[K+NY*(I0+I1*N0+I2*N0*N1)]=F\_k(X0[I0],X1[I1],X2[I2]), for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8270 \textcolor{comment}{                *  K=0...NY-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8271 \textcolor{comment}{                * I0=0...N0-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8272 \textcolor{comment}{                * I1=0...N1-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8273 \textcolor{comment}{                * I2=0...N2-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8274 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8275 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function supports weakly ordered grid nodes, i.e. you may  have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8276 \textcolor{comment}{      X[i]=X[i+1] for some i. It does  not  provide  you  any  performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8277 \textcolor{comment}{      benefits  due  to   duplication  of  points,  just  convenience  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8278 \textcolor{comment}{      flexibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8279 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8280 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this  function  is  re-\/entrant,  i.e.  you  may  use  same  rbfmodel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8281 \textcolor{comment}{      structure in multiple threads calling  this function  for  different}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8282 \textcolor{comment}{      grids.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8283 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8284 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: if you need function values on some subset  of  regular  grid, which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8285 \textcolor{comment}{      may be described as "{}several compact and  dense  islands"{},  you  may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8286 \textcolor{comment}{      use rbfgridcalc3vsubset().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8287 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8288 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8289 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 04.03.2016 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8290 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8334 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8335 \textcolor{comment}{    X2      -\/   array of grid nodes, third coordinates, array[N2]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8336 \textcolor{comment}{                Must be ordered by ascending. Exception is generated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8337 \textcolor{comment}{                if the array is not correctly ordered.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8338 \textcolor{comment}{    N2      -\/   grid size (number of nodes) in the third dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8339 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8340 \textcolor{comment}{    FlagY   -\/   array[N0*N1*N2]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8341 \textcolor{comment}{                * Y[I0+I1*N0+I2*N0*N1] corresponds to node (X0[I0],X1[I1],X2[I2])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8342 \textcolor{comment}{                * it is a "{}bitmap"{} array which contains  False  for  nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8343 \textcolor{comment}{                  which are NOT calculated, and True for nodes  which  are}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8345 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8349 \textcolor{comment}{                valued RBF models):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8350 \textcolor{comment}{                * Y[K+NY*(I0+I1*N0+I2*N0*N1)]=F\_k(X0[I0],X1[I1],X2[I2]),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8351 \textcolor{comment}{                  for K=0...NY-\/1, I0=0...N0-\/1, I1=0...N1-\/1, I2=0...N2-\/1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8352 \textcolor{comment}{                * elements of Y[] which correspond  to  FlagY[]=True   are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8353 \textcolor{comment}{                  loaded by model values (which may be  exactly  zero  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8354 \textcolor{comment}{                  some nodes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8355 \textcolor{comment}{                * elements of Y[] which correspond to FlagY[]=False MAY be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8356 \textcolor{comment}{                  initialized by zeros OR may be calculated. This function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8357 \textcolor{comment}{                  processes  grid  as  a  hierarchy  of  nested blocks and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8358 \textcolor{comment}{                  micro-\/rows. If just one element of micro-\/row is required,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8359 \textcolor{comment}{                  entire micro-\/row (up to 8 nodes in the current  version,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8360 \textcolor{comment}{                  but no promises) is calculated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8361 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8362 \textcolor{comment}{NOTE: this function supports weakly ordered grid nodes, i.e. you may  have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8363 \textcolor{comment}{      X[i]=X[i+1] for some i. It does  not  provide  you  any  performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8364 \textcolor{comment}{      benefits  due  to   duplication  of  points,  just  convenience  and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8365 \textcolor{comment}{      flexibility.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8377 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8378 \textcolor{comment}{This function "{}unpacks"{} RBF model by extracting its coefficients.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8379 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8380 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8381 \textcolor{comment}{    S       -\/   RBF model}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8382 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8383 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8384 \textcolor{comment}{    NX      -\/   dimensionality of argument}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8385 \textcolor{comment}{    NY      -\/   dimensionality of the target function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8386 \textcolor{comment}{    XWR     -\/   model information, array[NC,NX+NY+1].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8387 \textcolor{comment}{                One row of the array corresponds to one basis function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8388 \textcolor{comment}{                * first NX columns  -\/ coordinates of the center}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8389 \textcolor{comment}{                * next NY columns   -\/ weights, one per dimension of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8390 \textcolor{comment}{                                      function being modelled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8391 \textcolor{comment}{                For ModelVersion=1:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8392 \textcolor{comment}{                * last column       -\/ radius, same for all dimensions of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8393 \textcolor{comment}{                                      the function being modelled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8394 \textcolor{comment}{                For ModelVersion=2:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8395 \textcolor{comment}{                * last NX columns   -\/ radii, one per dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8396 \textcolor{comment}{    NC      -\/   number of the centers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8397 \textcolor{comment}{    V       -\/   polynomial  term , array[NY,NX+1]. One row per one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8398 \textcolor{comment}{                dimension of the function being modelled. First NX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8399 \textcolor{comment}{                elements are linear coefficients, V[NX] is equal to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8400 \textcolor{comment}{                constant part.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8401 \textcolor{comment}{    ModelVersion-\/version of the RBF model:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8402 \textcolor{comment}{                * 1 -\/ for models created by QNN and RBF-\/ML algorithms,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8403 \textcolor{comment}{                  compatible with ALGLIB 3.10 or earlier.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8404 \textcolor{comment}{                * 2 -\/ for models created by HierarchicalRBF, requires}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8405 \textcolor{comment}{                  ALGLIB 3.11 or later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8406 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8407 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/-\/ ALGLIB -\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8408 \textcolor{comment}{     Copyright 13.12.2011 by Bochkanov Sergey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8409 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{8450 }
\DoxyCodeLine{8451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{8452 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8453 \textcolor{comment}{This function  is  used  to  submit  a  request  for  termination  of  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8454 \textcolor{comment}{hierarchical RBF construction process from some other thread.  As  result,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8455 \textcolor{comment}{RBF construction is terminated smoothly (with proper deallocation  of  all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8456 \textcolor{comment}{necessary resources) and resultant model is filled by zeros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8457 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8458 \textcolor{comment}{A rep.terminationtype=8 will be returned upon receiving such request.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8459 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8460 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: only  HRBFs  (hierarchical  RBFs) support termination requests.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8461 \textcolor{comment}{           Legacy RBF-\/ML and RBF-\/QNN do not  support  it.  An  attempt  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8462 \textcolor{comment}{           terminate their construction will be ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8463 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8464 \textcolor{comment}{IMPORTANT: termination request flag is cleared when the model construction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8465 \textcolor{comment}{           starts. Thus, any pre-\/construction termination requests will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8466 \textcolor{comment}{           silently ignored -\/ only ones submitted AFTER  construction  has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8467 \textcolor{comment}{           actually began will be handled.}}
